style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">July&#160;23, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">, Forum Energy Technologies, Inc. (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Company</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;) issued a press release announcing earnings for the quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">. A copy of the release is furnished herewith as Exhibit&#160;99.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Exhibit 99.1 to this report contains &#8220;non-GAAP financial measures&#8221; as defined in Item 10 of Regulation S-K of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Exchange Act</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;). The non-GAAP financial measures reflect earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization expense (&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">EBITDA</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;) and adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income, adjusted net income per diluted share (&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Adjusted Diluted EPS</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;) and free cash flow, before acquisitions (&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">free cash flow</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;). A reconciliation of EBITDA, adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income, Adjusted Diluted EPS and free cash flow to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with Generally Accepted Accounting Principles in the United States (&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">GAAP</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8221;) is included as an attachment to the press release. The Company believes the presentation of EBITDA, adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income, Adjusted Diluted EPS and free cash flow is useful to the Company's investors because (i) EBITDA is an appropriate measure of evaluating the Company's operating performance and liquidity that reflects the resources available for strategic opportunities including, among others, investing in the business, strengthening the balance sheet, repurchasing the Company's securities and making strategic acquisitions and (ii) each of adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income, Adjusted Diluted EPS and free cash flow is useful to investors to assess and understand operating performance, especially when comparing those results with previous and subsequent periods or forecasting performance for future periods, primarily because management views the excluded items to be outside of the Company's normal operating results. In addition, EBITDA is a widely used benchmark in the investment community.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The presentation of this additional information is not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the Company's financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The information contained in <a name="sD4AC55DF1FE4CB4B0803347770CB6BF0"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;"><img src="fetlogoa01a01a01a01a01a02a01.jpg" style="height:58px;width:240px;"></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;padding-top:6px;text-align:center;font-size:16pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:16pt;font-weight:bold;">Forum Energy Technologies Announces </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;padding-top:6px;text-align:center;font-size:16pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:16pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter 2015 Results </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">HOUSTON, TEXAS, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">July&#160;23, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;- Forum Energy Technologies, Inc. (NYSE: FET) today announced </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2015 revenue of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$284 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$144 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">34%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, from the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2014. Net income for the quarter was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.10</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$40 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.41</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share for the prior year period. Excluding $0.06 per share of non-operational items, adjusted diluted earnings per share were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.16</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2015. Non-operational items for the quarter included primarily a foreign exchange loss</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">1</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and a restructuring charge. See Table I for a reconciliation of GAAP to non-GAAP financial information.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Second Quarter Results by Segment</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Drilling &amp; Subsea</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Drilling &amp; Subsea segment revenue in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2015 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$170 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$110 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">39%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, from the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2014. The revenue decline was due to lower drilling activity levels as reflected by the 51% drop in the North America land rig count for the same period. Additionally, reduced capital spending in the subsea sector impacted results compared to the prior year quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Production &amp; Infrastructure</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Production &amp; Infrastructure segment revenue in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2015 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$115 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$34 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">23%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, from the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter 2014. The reduction in North America completion activity resulted in lower sales of well site production equipment and pressure pumping consumable products from the prior year period. Partially offsetting the revenue decline was the addition of the J-Mac acquisition in the first quarter 2015. Sales of Forum&#8217;s valves were down only modestly compared to the prior year.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Review and Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Cris Gaut, Forum&#8217;s Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, remarked, "Forum second quarter revenue decreased 18% sequentially, primarily due to the continued decline in North America drilling and completion activity as the rig count dropped 40% from the first quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Our team implemented additional cost reduction measures and scaled down our business in line with declining activity levels. EBITDA for the quarter, excluding non-operational items, was $41 million, or 14.5% of revenue.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:5pt">1</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">&#32;Foreign exchange loss primarily relates to receivables billed in U.S. dollars by some of our non-U.S. subsidiaries that report in a local currency, and therefore the loss has no economic impact in dollar terms.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sD4AC55DF1FE4CB4B0803347770CB6BF0"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"We are focused on managing our cost structure and operating margins, reducing working capital and generating free cash flow as we enter the second half of the year.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Customer spending remains depressed in this low commodity price environment. New orders received by Forum in the second quarter were $198 million, a decline of 31% from the first quarter. Our second quarter 2015 book to bill ratio was 70%.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"We expect the lower level of new orders from the reduction in drilling and completion activity during the second quarter to have an impact on our third quarter results.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Forum expects diluted earnings per share for the third quarter 2015 of $0.08 to $0.13."</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Recent Events</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Forum&#8217;s joint venture company, Global Tubing, delivered the first order of coiled tubing for an onshore pipeline project. Coiled tubing pipeline is a continuously milled length of steel tubing that is coated and spooled for faster, lower cost and safer installations.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Conference Call Information</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Forum's conference call is scheduled for July 24, 2015 at 9:00 AM CDT. During the call, the Company intends to discuss second quarter 2015 results. To participate in the earnings conference call, please call 855-757-8876 within North America, or 631-485-4851 outside of North America. The access code is 73790835. The call will also be broadcast through the Investor Relations link on Forum&#8217;s website at www.f-e-t.com. Participants are encouraged to log in to the webcast or dial in to the conference call approximately ten minutes prior to the start time. A replay of the call will be available for two weeks after the call and may be accessed by dialing 855-859-2056 within&#160;North America, or 404-537-3406 outside of&#160;North America. The access code is 73790835.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sD4AC55DF1FE4CB4B0803347770CB6BF0"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;">Forum Energy Technologies&#160;is a global oilfield products company, serving the subsea, drilling, completion, production and infrastructure sectors of the oil and natural gas industry.&#160;The Company&#8217;s products include highly engineered capital equipment as well as products that are consumed in the drilling, well construction, production and transportation of oil and natural gas. Forum is headquartered in&#160;Houston, TX&#160;with manufacturing and distribution facilities strategically located around the globe.&#160;For more information, please visit www.f-e-t.com. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;padding-top:4px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward Looking Statements and Other Legal Disclosure</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This press release contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of Section 27A of the Securities Act of 1933 and Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:5pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:7pt;">&#160;The Company believes that the presentation of EBITDA, adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income and adjusted Diluted EPS is useful to the Company's investors because (i) EBITDA is an appropriate measure of evaluating the Company's operating performance and liquidity that reflects the resources available for strategic opportunities including, among others, investing in the business, strengthening the balance sheet, repurchasing the Company's securities and making strategic acquisitions and (ii) each of adjusted EBITDA, adjusted operating income and adjusted Diluted EPS is useful to investors to assess and understand operating performance, especially when comparing those results with previous and subsequent periods or forecasting performance for future periods, primarily because management views the excluded items to be outside of the Company's normal operating results. In addition, EBITDA is a widely used benchmark in the investment community.
